VENUES

create table venues (
	id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
	city VARCHAR(50),
	name VARCHAR(50),
	capacity INTEGER
);

TEAMS

create table teams (
	id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
	name VARCHAR(50),
	abbreviation VARCHAR(10),
	flag VARCHAR(500),
	wins INTEGER,
	draws INTEGER,
	losses INTEGER,
	scored_goals INTEGER,
	conceded_goals INTEGER,
	group_name VARCHAR(5),
	points INTEGER
);

COACHES

create table coaches (
	id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
	first_name VARCHAR(50),
	last_name VARCHAR(50),
	team_id INTEGER,
	FOREIGN KEY (team_id) REFERENCES teams(id)
);

PLAYERS

create table players (
	id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
	first_name VARCHAR(50),
	last_name VARCHAR(50),
	team_id INTEGER,
	minutes_played INTEGER,
	shirt_number INTEGER,
	yellow_cards INTEGER,
	red_cards INTEGER,
	available BOOLEAN,
	injured BOOLEAN,
	role VARCHAR(50),
	goals INTEGER,
	assists INTEGER,
	shots INTEGER,
	goals_saved INTEGER,
	goals_conceded INTEGER,
	FOREIGN KEY (team_id) REFERENCES teams(id)
);

GAMES

create table games (
	id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
	home_team_id INTEGER,
	away_team_id INTEGER,
	venue_id INTEGER,
	winner_id INTEGER,
	stage VARCHAR(50),
	spectators INTEGER,
	head_referee_id INTEGER,
	FOREIGN KEY (home_team_id) REFERENCES teams(id),
    	FOREIGN KEY (away_team_id) REFERENCES teams(id),
   	FOREIGN KEY (winner_id) REFERENCES teams(id),
    	FOREIGN KEY (head_referee_id) REFERENCES referees(id),
    	FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id)
);

CARDS

create table cards (
	id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
	game_id INTEGER,
	reciever INTEGER,
	referee_id INTEGER,
	minute_given INTEGER,
	card_color VARCHAR(50),
	FOREIGN KEY (referee_id) REFERENCES referees(id),
    	FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(id),
    	FOREIGN KEY (reciever) REFERENCES players(id)
);

SCHEDULE

create table schedule (
	id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
	date DATE,
	venue_id INTEGER,
	game_id INTEGER,
	FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(id),
    	FOREIGN KEY (venue_id) REFERENCES venues(id)
);

GOALS

create table goals (
	id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
	game_id INTEGER,
	scorer_id INTEGER,
	conceder_id INTEGER,
	assist_id INTEGER,
	minute_scored INTEGER,
	penalty BOOLEAN,
	shoot_out BOOLEAN,
	FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(id),
    	FOREIGN KEY (scorer_id) REFERENCES players(id),
    	FOREIGN KEY (conceder_id) REFERENCES players(id),
    	FOREIGN KEY (assist_id) REFERENCES players(id)
);
